# <a name="responsecode"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddd79-103">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddd79-103">ResponseCode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddd79-104">**ResponseCode**元素提供了有关请求的状态信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddd79-104">The **ResponseCode** element provides status information about the request.</span></span> 
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="ddd79-105">ResponseMessage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddd79-105">ResponseMessage</span></span>](responsemessage.md) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="ddd79-106">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddd79-106">ResponseCode</span></span>](responsecode.md)
  
```XML
<ResponseCode/>
```

<span data-ttu-id="ddd79-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddd79-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddd79-109">如下章节中介绍了属性、子元素和父元素。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddd79-109">The following sections describe attributes, child elements, and parent elements.</span></span>

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="ddd79-1480">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddd79-1480">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ddd79-1481">此元素不需要，并且不包含在所有响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddd79-1481">This element is not required and is not included in all responses.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="ddd79-1482">描述此元素的架构位于承载 Exchange Web Services 的 IIS 虚拟目录中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ddd79-1482">The schema that describes this element is located in the IIS virtual directory that hosts Exchange Web Services.</span></span>
